    <string name="_HY_RESULT_80_MESSAGE_MEDIUM_">"Your average blood pressure value is in the orange zone. Based on your results and the information you have given us, you should seek medical advice. As you are over 80 years of age, and especially if you are suffering from other disorders in addition to hypertension, your physician will assess whether or not you need a change in your treatment or medication.

It is possible that when your physician takes your blood pressure, he/she may have different values from yours. When your blood pressure is higher in a medical setting than at home, we call this the \"white coat effect\". In this case, only your physician can decide on the best treatment plan with you. \"Masked hypertension\" refers to a situation where normal blood pressure values are recorded in a medical setting and the home-measurement values are abnormal. According to some experts, masked hypertension may require stronger treatment. Future treatment adjustments should be made based on the average values calculated from a new series of self-measurements."</string>
